],\n  \"text\": \"Kafka's Java/Scala service initialization lifecycle is built around a small set of core abstractions:\\n\\n1. **`Server` trait** (`core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/Server.scala`): The top-level lifecycle interface defining `startup()`, `shutdown()`, and `awaitShutdown()`. It also defines the `ProcessStatus` sealed trait with states SHUTDOWN, STARTING, STARTED, and SHUTTING_DOWN that servers use to guard against concurrent state transitions.\\n\\n2. **`KafkaBroker` trait** (`core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/KafkaBroker.scala`): Extends the broker-specific lifecycle interface with `startup()`, `shutdown(timeout)`, `awaitShutdown()`, and `isShutdown()` along with accessor methods for all major broker subsystems.\\n\\n3. **`KafkaRaftServer`** (`core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/KafkaRaftServer.scala`): The concrete `Server` implementation for KRaft mode. Implements coordinated startup ordering: **controller starts first** (so it can handle broker registration), then broker. For shutdown: **broker shuts down first** (controlled shutdown via the controller), then controller. This reverse-order shutdown ensures dependent services stop before their dependencies.\\n\\n4. **`BrokerServer`** (`core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/BrokerServer.scala`): Implements `KafkaBroker`. Uses `maybeChangeStatus()` with the `ProcessStatus` enum to prevent concurrent startups or shutdowns. During shutdown, it performs a controlled shutdown by calling `replicaManager.beginControlledShutdown()` and `lifecycleManager.beginControlledShutdown()`, waiting for the controller to confirm partition leadership has been transferred before fully stopping.\\n\\n5. **`ControllerServer`** (`core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/ControllerServer.scala`): Implements the controller process lifecycle with the same `maybeChangeStatus()` pattern.\\n\\n6. **`BrokerLifecycleManager`** (`core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/BrokerLifecycleManager.scala`): Owns the broker state machine (registered, fenced, active, shutting down). Manages broker registration with the controller (KIP-631), periodic heartbeats, and the controlled shutdown sequence. Exposes `beginShutdown()` and `beginControlledShutdown()` to coordinate graceful shutdown. Uses an event queue to process state transitions sequentially.\\n\\n7. **`SharedServer`** (`core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/SharedServer.scala`): Manages components shared between BrokerServer and ControllerServer in combined mode (Raft manager, metadata loader, snapshot generator). Implements reference-counting start/stop via `startForBroker`/`startForController` and `stopForBroker`/`stopForController`, ensuring shared resources are only torn down when neither broker nor controller needs them.\\n\\n8. **`ShutdownableThread`** (`server-common/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/server/util/ShutdownableThread.java`): The foundational Java abstract class used throughout Kafka for worker threads. Provides `initiateShutdown()` (signals the thread to stop via a CountDownLatch and optional interrupt), `awaitShutdown()` (blocks until the thread completes), and `shutdown()` (combines both). Subclasses implement `doWork()` which is called in a loop until shutdown is initiated.\\n\\n9. **`Scheduler` interface / `KafkaScheduler`** (`server-common/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/server/util/Scheduler.java`, `KafkaScheduler.java`): Scheduler service with `startup()` and `shutdown()` lifecycle methods, used throughout the broker for periodic tasks.\\n\\n10. **`RaftManager`** (`core/src/main/scala/kafka/raft/RaftManager.scala`): The Raft consensus layer with `startup()` and `shutdown()` lifecycle methods.\\n\\n11. **`Kafka` object** (`core/src/main/scala/kafka/Kafka.scala`): The main entry point. Registers a JVM shutdown hook via `Exit.addShutdownHook` that calls `server.shutdown()` on SIGTERM/SIGINT, then calls `server.startup()` followed by `server.awaitShutdown()` to block the main thread until shutdown completes.\\n\\nThe coordinated shutdown sequence ensures dependent services stop in reverse startup order: broker stops first (performing a controlled shutdown to transfer partition leadership), then the controller stops, then the shared Raft/metadata infrastructure stops last.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":3652,"cache_read_input_tokens":50043,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":3652,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":8,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"dc06998f-9f23-4d2e-a79e-0e8d0fd40278","uuid":"d7b4d2db-b405-41dd-b65b-b75abf0ff232"}

(`core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/Server.scala`): The top-level lifecycle interface defining `startup()`, `shutdown()`, and `awaitShutdown()`. Also defines the `ProcessStatus` sealed trait with states SHUTDOWN, STARTING, STARTED, and SHUTTING_DOWN used by implementors to guard concurrent state transitions.\\n\\n2. **`KafkaBroker` trait** (`core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/KafkaBroker.scala`): Broker-specific lifecycle interface extending Logging, exposing `startup()`, `shutdown(timeout: Duration)`, `awaitShutdown()`, and `isShutdown()` along with accessors for all broker subsystems.\\n\\n3. **`KafkaRaftServer`** (`core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/KafkaRaftServer.scala`): The concrete `Server` implementation for KRaft mode. Implements the coordinated startup ordering: **controller starts first** (so it is ready to handle broker registration), then broker. For shutdown, **broker shuts down first** (to perform controlled shutdown with the controller), then controller—reverse startup order.\\n\\n4. **`BrokerServer`** (`core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/BrokerServer.scala`): Implements `KafkaBroker`. Uses `maybeChangeStatus()` with `ProcessStatus` to prevent concurrent lifecycle transitions. During shutdown, calls `replicaManager.beginControlledShutdown()` and `lifecycleManager.beginControlledShutdown()`, waits for the controller to confirm partition leadership transfer, then tears down subsystems in reverse startup order.\\n\\n5. **`ControllerServer`** (`core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/ControllerServer.scala`): Implements the controller process lifecycle with the same `maybeChangeStatus()` state machine pattern.\\n\\n6. **`BrokerLifecycleManager`** (`core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/BrokerLifecycleManager.scala`): Owns the broker state machine (registering, fenced, active, controlled shutdown). Manages broker registration with the controller (KIP-631) and periodic heartbeats. Exposes `beginShutdown()` and `beginControlledShutdown()` to coordinate graceful shutdown. Uses an event queue for sequential state transitions.\\n\\n7. **`SharedServer`** (`core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/SharedServer.scala`): Manages components shared between BrokerServer and ControllerServer in combined mode (Raft manager, metadata loader, snapshot generator). Implements reference-style start/stop via `startForBroker`/`startForController` and `stopForBroker`/`stopForController`—shared resources are only stopped when neither server needs them.\\n\\n8. **`ShutdownableThread`** (`server-common/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/server/util/ShutdownableThread.java`): The foundational abstract Java class for all Kafka worker threads. Provides `initiateShutdown()` (signals the thread via CountDownLatch and optional interrupt), `awaitShutdown()` (blocks until the thread exits), and `shutdown()` (combines both). Subclasses implement `doWork()` called in a loop until shutdown is initiated.\\n\\n9. **`Scheduler` interface / `KafkaScheduler`** (`server-common/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/server/util/Scheduler.java`, `KafkaScheduler.java`): A task scheduler service with `startup()` and `shutdown()` lifecycle methods used throughout the broker for periodic background tasks.\\n\\n10. **`RaftManager` / `KafkaRaftManager`** (`core/src/main/scala/kafka/raft/RaftManager.scala`): The Raft consensus layer with `startup()` and `shutdown()` lifecycle methods, started and stopped by SharedServer.\\n\\n11. **`Kafka` object** (`core/src/main/scala/kafka/Kafka.scala`): The main entry point. Builds a `KafkaRaftServer`, registers a JVM shutdown hook via `Exit.addShutdownHook` that calls `server.shutdown()` on SIGTERM/SIGINT, calls `server.startup()`, then blocks on `server.awaitShutdown()`.\\n\\nThe key design pattern is reverse-order shutdown: components that start last are stopped first, ensuring that dependent services (broker) stop before their dependencies (controller, Raft layer, shared infrastructure). The `BrokerLifecycleManager` adds a coordinated controlled-shutdown phase where the broker notifies the controller to transfer partition leadership before stopping, minimizing disruption to producers and consumers.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":3,"cache_creation_input_tokens":374,"cache_read_input_tokens":56874,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":374,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"dc06998f-9f23-4d2e-a79e-0e8d0fd40278","uuid":"3d25e726-6c6f-4f54-92cd-643e00003152"}
